Chapter 1500: Trading with the Bone Race Again!

Chapter 1500: Trading with the Bone Race Again!

Ye Tian did not concern himself with the matter of the fourth Dark Holy Land.
Ultimately, a portion of the fourth Dark Holy Land's territory was occupied by the human race, and other forces did not dare to say anything.
Even if the human race were to completely occupy the fourth Holy Land, the other Ancestors would have nothing to say; after all, the human race was indeed too powerful.
......
"My cultivation progress is getting slower and slower!"
Ye Tian said helplessly.
Although his duplicated bodies were still working hard to collect resources from the Saint Realm, it was still not enough for his use.
Consequently, the cultivation speed of his main body was becoming slower and slower, and many resources were now almost useless to him, making it difficult to increase his strength.
"Perhaps I can try trading with the Bone Race!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
The Bone Race was very powerful and possessed countless resources. If he traded with them, he could obtain many precious resources that would be very helpful in increasing his strength.
On this day.
Ye Tian's main body personally descended upon the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
When Ye Tian appeared in the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, the entire area began to tremble.
Immediately, the experts of the Bone Race fell into a state of panic.
"A Supreme Ancestor!!!!"
They were terrified.
A Supreme Ancestor was a powerful existence capable of rivaling a Bone Emperor; they had no way to resist.
Furthermore, the Bone Emperor was about to descend, and his strength would be reduced, so he might not necessarily be able to contend with a Supreme Ancestor.
This was a true disaster!
Of course, many members of the Bone Race also recognized Ye Tian. He was the top-tier Ancestor who had invaded the Bone Sea Forbidden Land multiple times many ages ago, but now he had ascended to the rank of Supreme Ancestor.
"Respected Supreme Ancestor, you signed an agreement with our Bone Emperor not to invade the Bone Sea Forbidden Land again!" a Bone King said, suppressing the terror in his heart.
"I am not here to make an enemy of your Bone Race; I have simply come to discuss a trade!"
Ye Tian spoke.
A trade?
Many experts of the Bone Race were filled with doubt, not knowing what Ye Tian wanted to trade.
In the past, they had never traded with the Ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Domain because, in their eyes, the creatures of the Dark Forbidden Domain were mere ants to be slaughtered at will.
When the day of the Great Calamity arrived, what resources would they not have? Everything would be theirs to harvest. Therefore, they looked down on the weak Ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Domain and naturally would not trade with them.
Moreover, trading was equivalent to strengthening the power of the Dark Forbidden Domain. If a large number of top-tier Ancestors were born, wouldn't they be creating trouble for themselves?
Thus, experts from other foreign worlds would not trade with the Ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Domain unless the Dark Forbidden Domain could produce something so good that the foreign experts could not refuse.
But now that Ye Tian had stepped into the Supreme Ancestor realm, he naturally had the qualifications to trade with the Bone Race.
"Respected Supreme Ancestor, allow us to report this to the Bone Emperor. We cannot make decisions regarding trade!"
The Bone King said hurriedly.
"Very well!"
Ye Tian nodded.
He wasn't planning to trade with these Bone Kings anyway; mere Bone Kings couldn't produce anything truly good, and they wouldn't be of much help to him.
After all, with his current Supreme Ancestor realm, even Bone King Marrow Beads were of little help to him.
Before long, a wisp of the Bone Emperor's consciousness passed through the portal and arrived at the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
This conscious avatar did not possess much power, but the cost to send it was small. Since he wasn't here to fight, there was no need to pay the massive price to descend with his true body.
"What business do you have with me?"
The Bone Emperor of the Bone Race asked indifferently, though he was inwardly shocked.
Back then, he wasn't surprised that Ye Tian could cultivate to the peak of the top-tier Ancestor level. Although Ye Tian's combat power was astonishing and he had created so many Ultimate Ancestral Defensive Techniques, as long as he couldn't step into the Supreme Ancestor realm, he could not be compared to an existence like himself.
But how much time had passed? Ye Tian had actually stepped into the Supreme Ancestor realm, and judging by his aura, he hadn't just broken through; he had already stabilized his realm long ago.
Breaking through to the Supreme Ancestor realm was not something that could be achieved through bitter cultivation alone. One had to leave the Dark Forbidden Domain, travel to another foreign world, comprehend the rules of that world, and then walk the path of that foreign world. Only by merging the two paths could one break the shackles and step into the Supreme Ancestor realm.
He didn't know how many gates the Dark Forbidden Domain had.
Perhaps Ye Tian got lucky and passed through a gate, and the foreign world on the other side just happened to be in the midst of a Great Calamity.
Regardless of the situation, it was enough to prove that Ye Tian's luck and talent were both incredibly heaven-defying; otherwise, he could not have stepped into the Supreme Ancestor realm.
Now that Ye Tian had reached the Supreme Ancestor realm, at least within the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, the Bone Race could no longer do anything to him.
"I wish to trade some resources with the Bone Race. I know that the resources of the Dark Forbidden Domain are very useful to your Bone Race, and similarly, some of your Bone Race's resources are very helpful to me. Wouldn't it be better for us to trade with each other?" Ye Tian suggested.
"Our Bone Race is currently not lacking in resources!"
The Bone Emperor intended to refuse.
He did not want to strengthen the power of the Dark Forbidden Domain; it brought him no benefit.
"Bone Emperor, don't be so quick to refuse. I presume the Bone Race is unwilling to offend a Supreme Ancestor? Furthermore, I am willing to use resources from the Dark Forbidden Domain as well as resources from other foreign worlds to trade with the Bone Race. Additionally, I have already taken over another foreign world. Although it is a very weak one, the Dark Forbidden Domain will birth more Supreme Ancestors in the future. While I have signed an agreement with your Bone Race and will not act against the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, others have not signed such an agreement. If the Bone Race is willing to trade with me, I can guarantee that other Supreme Ancestors will not lay a hand on the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, and its existence can be preserved permanently. How about it?" Ye Tian proposed.
"What? Your Dark Forbidden Domain has already taken over a foreign world?"
The Bone Emperor found it hard to believe.
However, it was certain that the Dark Forbidden Domain had at least established a base in another foreign world; otherwise, it would have been impossible for Ye Tian to break through to the Supreme Ancestor realm.
It was foreseeable that the Dark Forbidden Domain would definitely birth more Supreme Ancestors in the future.
If that were truly the case, the Dark Forbidden Domain could indeed completely destroy the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
Now, suppressing the rise of the Dark Forbidden Domain was no longer possible; it was better to trade with them.
"Fine, I agree!"
The Bone Emperor responded.
Next, Ye Tian traded with this Bone Emperor of the Bone Race.
The Bone Emperor brought out many resources, and Ye Tian refined and tested them one by one, only trading for resources that were significantly helpful to him.
After a round of trading, Ye Tian brought out a massive amount of Dark Forbidden Domain resources. Since these resources were of little help to him—one could even say they were useless—it was essentially recycling waste.
In exchange, he obtained a massive amount of useful resources from the Bone Race, and the same was true for the Bone Race.
Finally.
"Bone Emperor, does your Bone Race possess any cultivation secrets regarding the Bone Emperor level? I have only just stepped into the Supreme Ancestor realm and do not understand this level very well. If you have any, I can offer some resources in exchange," Ye Tian asked.
"I can, but I will only trade some basic information with you. As for truly useful secrets, I will not trade those," the Bone Emperor said.
Soon after, Ye Tian used some resources to trade for a manual from the Bone Emperor. This manual was naturally inscribed by the Bone Emperor on the spot, and it recorded some information regarding the Bone Emperor level.
Whether it was a Bone Emperor or a Supreme Ancestor, they were actually at the same level and naturally shared common points.
With the trade completed, Ye Tian happily left the Bone Sea Forbidden Land and returned to the Profound Void Ancestral World.

Chapter 1501: The Three Levels of Supreme Ancestors!

Chapter 1501: The Three Levels of Supreme Ancestors!

Ye Tian was in no hurry to refine the resources from the Bone Race; instead, he began studying the manual obtained from the Bone Emperor.
This manual recorded some information regarding the Bone Emperors, such as their classifications.
The cultivation of a Bone Emperor was generally divided into three levels. The first level consisted of those who had just broken through to become a Bone Emperor. Although such a Bone Emperor was much stronger than a Bone King, the difference wasn't overly exaggerated. If there were enough Bone Kings, it was even possible to wear down and kill a first-level Bone Emperor.
The second level consisted of Bone Emperors who had mastered a Supreme Ancestral Technique. The Bone Race also practiced Ancestral Techniques, and their terminology was similar.
An Ultimate Ancestral Technique was almost the most powerful technique in a given world, representing the "ultimate," or the limit.
However, above Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, there were still Supreme Ancestral Techniques. The manual did not mention the secrets of Supreme Ancestral Techniques or how to cultivate them; after all, the Bone Emperor would not teach Ye Tian how to cultivate a Supreme Ancestral Technique.
In short, a Bone Emperor who mastered a Supreme Ancestral Technique and raised their cultivation to a certain level could be ranked in the second level.
Then there was the third level, which belonged to the peak realm of Bone Emperors. They mastered multiple Supreme Ancestral Techniques, and their cultivation had reached the absolute limit, unable to advance further, standing only a single step away from the next realm.
Above the Bone Emperor was the Bone Saint, a classification equivalent to the invincible Ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Zone.
"I should still belong to the first level of Supreme Ancestors. I must master a Supreme Ancestral Technique before I can step into the second level. However, my foundation is extremely deep, and I cultivate the Endless Ancestor Path, so my true combat power should be close to the second level!" Ye Tian thought to himself.
He had some guesses about how to master a Supreme Ancestral Technique, but he wasn't certain.
"In the future, I'll have my cloned body, the He Yuan Holy Beast, consult the two Supreme Holy Beasts of the Sea Sky Holy Sect. They might know!" Ye Tian murmured.
In the following days, Ye Tian began refining the resources from the Bone Race, and his strength continued to improve.
In the blink of an eye, several Realm Eras passed in the Dark Forbidden Zone.
By this time, Ye Tian had long since finished refining the resources from the Bone Race. He wanted to trade with them again, but unfortunately, the Bone Race began to act perfunctorily. Consequently, he couldn't trade for many resources from them. On the other hand, from the Sea Sky Holy Sect's side, his cloned body would send over resources from time to time, ensuring he never lacked cultivation materials.
Additionally, he frequently sent resources from the Dark Forbidden Zone to his cloned body, the He Yuan Holy Beast, for cultivation. As a result, the strength of this cloned body improved quite rapidly and was now not far from the limit of a top-tier Holy Beast.
One day.
Ye Tian's cloned body, the He Yuan Holy Beast, went to visit one of the Supreme Holy Beasts of the Sea Sky Holy Sect—the Wolf Bone Holy Beast.
"Greetings, Lord Wolf Bone Holy Beast!"
Ye Tian's cloned body, the He Yuan Holy Beast, said respectfully.
"He Yuan, why have you come to see me?"
The Wolf Bone Holy Beast asked.
"I wish to ask Lord Wolf Bone Holy Beast a few questions," Ye Tian said.
"Speak, what is it?"
The Wolf Bone Holy Beast said indifferently.
"Lord Wolf Bone Holy Beast, I want to know how one can comprehend a Supreme Holy Technique!"
Ye Tian asked.
"Holy Technique" was the term used in the Holy Realm for Ancestral Techniques; a Holy Technique here was equivalent to an Ancestral Technique in the Dark Forbidden Zone.
And a Supreme Holy Technique was equivalent to a Supreme Ancestral Technique.
Upon hearing the name "Supreme Holy Technique," the Wolf Bone Holy Beast's voice turned cold. "He Yuan, this is not knowledge you should be concerned with. You are merely a top-tier Holy Beast. You will find out once you step into the rank of Supreme Holy Beast."
"Lord Wolf Bone Holy Beast, I am merely curious,"
Ye Tian hurriedly said.
Afterward, under his persistent requests, the Wolf Bone Holy Beast finally spoke: "There is no harm in telling you. To comprehend a Supreme Holy Technique, one must go to an Otherworld to comprehend an Ultimate Holy Technique of the same type, and then fuse our Holy Realm's Ultimate Holy Technique with the Otherworld's similar Ultimate Holy Technique. It is the same method as breaking through to become a Supreme Holy Beast. However, if one cannot step into the level of a Supreme Holy Beast, there is no way to fuse two Ultimate Holy Techniques."
"Lord Wolf Bone Holy Beast, once two Ultimate Holy Techniques from different worlds are fused, can one break the shackles of Ultimate Holy Techniques and comprehend a Supreme Holy Technique?" Ye Tian asked excitedly.
"Correct!" The Wolf Bone Holy Beast nodded. "However, in our Holy Realm, only one Supreme Holy Beast has ever comprehended a Supreme Holy Technique. You should put such thoughts out of your mind!"
"Yes!"
Ye Tian nodded and then withdrew.
...
"From the information obtained from the Wolf Bone Holy Beast, the Holy Realm likely only has one Supreme Holy Beast at the second level. No, that Supreme Holy Beast who comprehended a Supreme Holy Technique might have even reached the third level. However, the strength of the Holy Realm is still not that great. Once I become stronger in the future, there is a high hope of completely occupying this Holy Realm," Ye Tian thought to himself.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian's cloned body began a period of secluded meditation to comprehend and create an Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
The Ultimate Ancestral Technique he prepared to create was the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique. Once he created the Holy Realm's version of the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique, he could fuse it with the Dark Forbidden Zone's version, giving him hope of fusing them into the Supreme Ancestral Technique: Overlord Strength.
At that time, his strength would receive a terrifying boost, instantly stepping into the second level of Supreme Ancestors.
However, this cloned body did not possess the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent. Trying to create the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique would be extremely difficult.
He could spend a vast amount of time creating and comprehending it, but it might take more than a single Dark Era. By then, he wouldn't be able to step into the second level of Supreme Ancestors before the Great Tribulation of the Holy Realm.
"I'll first bestow the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent to the cloned body. Once the cloned body creates the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique, I'll take the talent back."
Ye Tian planned.
But this plan carried a risk: a bestowed talent could not be replicated. This meant Ye Tian would temporarily lose the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent. If the cloned body, the He Yuan Holy Beast, were to perish, he would lose the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent forever.
In that case, he would have to search for a large number of Strength Ancestral Talents to replicate and slowly fuse them back into an Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent, which would undoubtedly waste a lot of his time, and he might not even be able to obtain it again.
However, compared to the potential gains, it was worth the risk.
One day.
Ye Tian's cloned body entered the Sea Sky Forbidden Land once again. Subsequently, his main body infiltrated the Sea Sky Forbidden Land, instantly bestowed the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent to the cloned body, and then the main body left the forbidden land.
Having obtained the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent, the cloned body He Yuan Holy Beast's comprehension for creating a Strength-type Ultimate Ancestral Technique increased many times over.
Next, Ye Tian's cloned body remained in the Sea Sky Forbidden Land to comprehend the laws of strength of this world and create the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
With the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent as an aid, the cloned body's speed of comprehension was very fast.
He estimated that it wouldn't be long before he could create the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
As expected.
In just ten Realm Years, the cloned body successfully created the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
If he hadn't had the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent, he would likely have needed countless times more time to create it.
He did not enter the Sea Sky Forbidden Land again immediately, as too short an interval would arouse suspicion.
After several Realm Eras had passed, Ye Tian's cloned body finally applied to enter the Sea Sky Forbidden Land.
Once the cloned body returned to the Sea Sky Forbidden Land, memories were shared. Ye Tian's main body naturally obtained the cloned body's memories and the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique from the Holy Realm.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian's main body infiltrated the Sea Sky Forbidden Land again, stripped the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent from the cloned body, and reclaimed the talent.
Thus, Ye Tian's plan was complete.
With two versions of the Overlord Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique in hand, once they were fused, he would be able to step into the second level of Supreme Ancestors.

Chapter 1502: Another Breakthrough, the Second Level of the Ultimate Ancestor!

Chapter 1502: Another Breakthrough, the Second Level of the Ultimate Ancestor!

After obtaining the two Overpowering Paramount Ancestral Techniques, Ye Tian began to work hard on merging them.
In reality, the essence of the two Paramount Ancestral Techniques was the same; they simply aligned with different laws of heaven and earth.
One belonged to the laws of the Dark Forbidden Zone, and the other belonged to the laws of the Sanctuary World.
Therefore, merging these two Paramount Ancestral Techniques was not an easy task.
As time slowly passed, Ye Tian gradually grasped the mysteries of the fusion.
First of all, to merge these two Paramount Ancestral Techniques, they had to be tailored to oneself, fused based on his own being.
For example, even if he merged these two Paramount Ancestral Techniques to create an Ultimate Ancestral Technique, and his cloned body, the Heyuan Sacred Beast, obtained the memories of that Ultimate Ancestral Technique, the clone would still be unable to perform it. This was unless the cloned body also merged two Paramount Sacred Arts that suited its own body to break through the shackles and comprehend an Ultimate Sacred Art.
The cloned body, the Heyuan Sacred Beast, was currently not even an Ultimate Sacred Beast, so it naturally had no way to comprehend an Ultimate Sacred Art.
However, Ye Tian was now thinking of helping the cloned body, the Heyuan Sacred Beast, break through its shackles and promote it to an Ultimate Sacred Beast.
Of course, he had to wait until his main body stepped into the second level of the Ultimate Ancestor before helping the cloned body break through.
In fact, he didn't really need to waste time doing this. After all, once his main body reached the Ultimate Ancestor realm, he could simply clone the body of an Ultimate Sacred Beast.
But Ye Tian felt that if the cloned body achieved a self-breakthrough to become an Ultimate Sacred Beast, it might be like when Ancestor Qingye broke through—the cloned body might become permanently fixed as an avatar and no longer occupy a slot for cloned bodies.
If that were the case, it would be equivalent to having an extra permanent avatar at the Ultimate Sacred Beast level.
This was an attempt; if it truly failed, it would merely be a waste of some time.
One Domain Era after another passed.
Unknowingly, nearly a hundred Domain Eras had gone by, almost a full Dark Era, and by this time, the Great Tribulation of the Sanctuary World was approaching.
On this day.
Ye Tian was finally about to comprehend an Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
"It's so difficult. I didn't expect that merging two Overpowering Paramount Ancestral Techniques would be even harder than breaking through to become an Ultimate Ancestor. I thought that with my realm as an Ultimate Ancestor, it wouldn't take long to merge them, but it actually took nearly a full Dark Era."
Ye Tian said with some surprise.
However, he finally comprehended it.
Boom!!!!
The two Overpowering Paramount Ancestral Techniques merged, transforming into an Overpowering Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
The moment the Overpowering Ultimate Ancestral Technique was successfully comprehended, a terrifying power surged within Ye Tian's body.
At this moment, Ye Tian's physical strength began to skyrocket, comparable to the transformation when he broke through from a Top-tier Ancestor to an Ultimate Ancestor.
The transformation of his power caused his body to continuously absorb energy from the outside world, but this energy was still not enough.
Thus, Ye Tian used all the energy he had collected during this period to complete the power transformation.
It took several Domain Years for this transformation to be completely finished.
"I didn't expect that comprehending an Ultimate Ancestral Technique would actually trigger a transformation of power. My current strength has increased by too much!"
Ye Tian clenched his fist, and the void itself began to shatter. He couldn't help but feel astonished.
At this moment, he finally understood why the Ultimate Ancestors were divided into three levels. Once one comprehends an Ultimate Ancestral Technique, they belong to the second level.
After all, once an Ultimate Ancestral Technique is mastered—no matter which kind it is—one's strength will skyrocket to a terrifying degree.
"With my strength soaring, if I perform the Overpowering Ultimate Ancestral Technique again, my attack power will far exceed what it was before. Even an ordinary Ultimate Ancestor or Ultimate Sacred Beast would likely be heavily wounded by a single strike from me!" Ye Tian thought to himself.
At this point, there were only a few Domain Eras left until the Sanctuary World's tribulation.
By now, all the major forces in the Sanctuary World were preparing for this Great Tribulation.
After Ye Tian stabilized his realm, he began to create a Sacred Art based on the body of his clone, the Heyuan Sacred Beast.
Ye Tian's cloned body, the Heyuan Sacred Beast, had promoted to a Sacred Beast using the Six-Armed Vajra Technique, and this Sacred Art had also been dedicated to the Haitian Sacred Sect.
Later, Ye Tian found this Sacred Art in the Haitian Sacred Sect's Sacred Art Treasury; otherwise, there really would have been no way to charge toward the Ultimate Sacred Beast level.
Now that he had the Sacred Art for the cloned body, he just needed to create a Sacred Art that aligned with the laws of the Dark Forbidden Zone.
Ye Tian's main body's realm was extremely high, having stepped into the second level of the Ultimate Ancestor, so creating a version of the Six-Armed Vajra Technique that suited the Dark Forbidden Zone was not very difficult.
It only took a dozen or so Domain Years for Ye Tian to successfully create the Dark Forbidden Zone version of the Six-Armed Vajra Technique.
Shortly after.
The cloned body, the Heyuan Sacred Beast, arrived at the Haitian Forbidden Land. It instantly shared memories with the main body, obtained this Six-Armed Vajra Technique, and then returned to the Haitian Sacred Sect.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian's cloned body began practicing the Six-Armed Vajra Technique from the Dark Forbidden Zone, using this Sacred Art to charge toward becoming a Sacred Beast of the second path.
Soon, the second path also stepped into the Sacred Beast level.
The countless resources Ye Tian had collected from the Dark Forbidden Zone had long been delivered to the cloned body. Now, the cloned body used these resources to cultivate rapidly. The second path progressed quickly, stepping into the Top-tier Sacred Beast level, and then rapidly advanced to the limit of a Top-tier Sacred Beast.
With both paths having reached the limit of a Top-tier Sacred Beast, it meant that this cloned body of Ye Tian's could now attempt to break through to the Ultimate Sacred Beast level.
Normally, merging two Sacred Arts would take at least dozens of Domain Eras, but these two Sacred Arts were far inferior to the Endless Ancestor Law, so the difficulty of fusion was not high.
Additionally, Ye Tian's current realm was very high—he was a second-level Ultimate Ancestor. Although the cloned body's realm was still at the Top-tier Sacred Beast level, it possessed the memories of the main body. Therefore, in terms of insight and comprehension, it far surpassed any Top-tier Sacred Beast.
Thus, Ye Tian felt he had hope to completely elevate this cloned body to the Ultimate Sacred Beast level within the next few Domain Eras—specifically, before the day the Great Tribulation arrived.
"Let's begin!"
Ye Tian devoted all his efforts to comprehension, working hard to merge the two Sacred Arts.
One Domain Year after another flowed by, and unknowingly, one Domain Era passed.
At this point, Ye Tian felt his comprehension was nearly complete. Perhaps with one more Domain Era of cultivation, he would be certain of completely merging the two Sacred Arts.
Finally, another Domain Era passed.
On this day, Ye Tian completely merged the two Sacred Arts, and the two Sacred Beast bodies also began to fuse, transforming toward an Ultimate Sacred Beast body.
Haitian Sacred Sect.
The gazes of two Ultimate Sacred Beasts pierced through infinite space simultaneously, looking toward the place where the Heyuan Sacred Beast was in seclusion.
"What's happening? The Heyuan Sacred Beast is breaking through? He's about to step into the Ultimate Sacred Beast level?"
The two Ultimate Sacred Beasts were dumbfounded.

Chapter 1503: Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals!

Chapter 1503: Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals!

Not only were the two Supreme Saint Beasts of the Sea-Sky Saint Sect stunned, but the other Saint Beasts were also dumbfounded.
He Yuan Saint Beast had been very low-key for the past few Dark Eras, with little presence, and had shown almost no signs of a breakthrough. How did he suddenly break through?
One must know that many Saint Beasts had better talent than He Yuan Saint Beast and faster cultivation speeds, and had reached the limit of Top-tier Saint Beasts long ago, even entering the Dark Forbidden Zone twice, yet they still hadn't broken through.
On what basis did He Yuan Saint Beast break through?
Immediately, some Top-tier Saint Beasts became jealous.
Of course, many disciples and some Saint Beasts of the Sea-Sky Saint Sect were still very excited. After all, the addition of a Supreme Saint Beast to the Sea-Sky Saint Sect meant the sect's strength had grown even greater, and their lives would naturally be much easier.
Furthermore, the Great Tribulation was approaching. The stronger the Sea-Sky Saint Sect was, the more hope they had of survival.
After all, the Great Tribulation was terrifying, and for the Sea-Sky Saint Sect, it was also a massive challenge.
"Ensure He Yuan Saint Beast's safety, and do not let anyone disturb—him!"
The two Supreme Saint Beasts, Wolf Bone Saint Beast and Violent Ape Saint Beast, ordered.
However, they had no idea that this was not their Sea-Sky Saint Sect's He Yuan Saint Beast, but merely Ye Tian's duplicated body. If they knew, they would definitely kill Ye Tian's duplicated body at any cost.
As time passed, combined with the refining of a large amount of resources, Ye Tian's duplicated body continued to transform, its physique becoming stronger and stronger.
After a long period of time, the Supreme Saint Beast body of Ye Tian's duplicated body, He Yuan Saint Beast, had completely finished its transformation.
At this point, this duplicated body had stepped into the Supreme Saint Beast realm.
When the duplicated body He Yuan Saint Beast stepped into the Supreme Saint Beast realm, it actually established a faint connection with the main body.
Previously, the duplicated body was too weak, and the connection could not cross the Gate. Thus, there was no way to connect with the main body; every time, it had to pass through the Gate and enter the Sea-Sky Forbidden Land before it could contact the main body.
But now, there was no need to worry.
"The connection is very faint, but at least I can connect. It only takes about several decades to connect once!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Soon, several decades passed, and the duplicated body connected with the main body once.
The moment they connected, the Duplication Talent underwent a change; strictly speaking, the ability of the duplicated body changed.
"I can re-solidify a duplicated body?"
Ye Tian was somewhat surprised.
Previously, his duplicated body, Ancestor Qing Ye, did not occupy a duplicated body slot and was permanently solidified as a special clone.
Unfortunately, this clone had disregarded its foundation for the sake of promotion back then and had fused with someone else's Ancestral Law. Thus, its potential was very limited. Although it had now reached the level of a Top-tier Ancestor, wanting to advance to a Supreme Ancestor would be a hundred times more difficult than for others.
Therefore, this clone's potential was lacking, and it was no longer of much use.
After all, in the Dark Forbidden Zone, Ye Tian's main body could suppress everything. What use was a mere Top-tier Ancestor clone? It wasn't even as useful as an incarnation.
"Then I'll give up the Ancestor Qing Ye clone and make He Yuan Saint Beast the permanently solidified clone. That way, my main body can free up the duplicated body slot, allowing me to use duplicated bodies repeatedly and burn Ancestral Souls to comprehend Ultimate Ancestral Techniques and fuse Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. My cultivation speed will increase many times over!"
Ye Tian planned.
*Crack!!!!*
Dark Soul Domain.
Ancestor Qing Ye's clone shattered, and its aura dissipated.
Immediately, the Ancestors of the Human Race sensed it and became panicked.
But soon, Ye Tian sent a message, which calmed the Human Race's Ancestors.
With the dissipation of the Ancestor Qing Ye clone, He Yuan Saint Beast, far away in the Sea-Sky Saint Sect of the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth, became the permanently solidified clone.
At this moment, Ye Tian finally breathed a sigh of relief.
"The duplicated body doesn't need to be maintained constantly; in the future, it can be used as a consumable to constantly overdraw potential to comprehend Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. With the Evolution ability and the continuously condensing duplicated bodies, I can definitely comprehend a second Supreme Ancestral Technique in a short time. Of course, the prerequisite is to first occupy the Sea-Sky Saint Sect; otherwise, I won't be able to comprehend the rules in the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth in peace."
Ye Tian murmured.
Before long, only several decades remained before the Great Tribulation of the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth.
-----------------
Saint Realm Heaven and Earth, Sea-Sky Saint Sect.
Ye Tian's clone, He Yuan Saint Beast, was with Wolf Bone Saint Beast and Violent Ape Saint Beast, discussing the time of the Great Tribulation.
At this time, Ye Tian had just come out of seclusion, so he didn't understand many things.
"The Great Tribulation is coming; this time, our Saint Realm Heaven and Earth will face great trouble," the Violent Ape Saint Beast lamented.
Ye Tian didn't say much; after all, he wasn't the real He Yuan Saint Beast, and it wouldn't be good if he said the wrong thing.
Therefore, he only listened, occasionally speaking up to say some unimportant words.
Gradually, Ye Tian gained some understanding of this Great Tribulation.
The Great Tribulation faced by the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth was not as terrifying as the one in the Dark Forbidden Zone. The Dark Forbidden Zone was too weak; during the first three Great Tribulations, there was no resistance at all. Even Top-tier Ancestors would hide and not dare to show their faces, allowing experts from other foreign realms to plunder resources.
· ········· Seeking Flowers ··· ·····
But the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth was different. The Saint Realm Heaven and Earth possessed Supreme Saint Beasts, and more than one. It even had a Supreme Saint Beast of the second level, so it naturally had a certain degree of resistance.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian spoke up: "Wolf Bone Saint Beast, Violent Ape Saint Beast, why not destroy those Gates in the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth? Top-tier Ancestors find it hard to invade those forbidden lands, but we Supreme Saint Beasts should have enough strength to destroy their forbidden lands and shatter their Gates, right?"
Wolf Bone Saint Beast smiled and said: "He Yuan Saint Beast, you've just broken through to the Supreme Saint Beast level, so you don't understand some things. True, we do have the strength to destroy a forbidden land, but those forces have already locked onto the coordinate position of the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth and can establish a Gate again. When they establish a Gate next time, I'm afraid they will seek frantic revenge. Moreover, destroying a Gate is not simple. Gates are divided into three tiers. A First-tier Gate is the weakest and only allows Top-tier Saint Beasts to enter; Supreme Saint Beasts can also pass through by paying a price, but it will cause damage to the Gate and require many resources to repair. A Second-tier Gate allows Supreme Saint Beasts to pass, and even Invincible Saint Beasts can enter by paying a price. A Third-tier Gate is the legendary Gate, comparable to a Gate naturally born between heaven and earth; that kind of Gate allows Invincible Saint Beasts to enter, and even Peerless Saint Beasts can pass through by paying a price."
... .. 0
"Is our Sea-Sky Saint Sect's Gate a First-tier Gate?"
Ye Tian asked.
"Yes!" Wolf Bone Saint Beast nodded. "We don't have the construction method for a Second-tier Gate, but the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth does have one Second-tier Gate. The force corresponding to that Second-tier Gate is terrifying; the three Great Saint Sects alone cannot stop them. Therefore, our three Great Saint Sects have allied with some foreign forces. we won't destroy their Gates, but during the Great Tribulation, they need to join forces with us to resist the force where that Second-tier Gate is located. This is the ultimate reason why we don't destroy some Gates."
"So that's how it is!"
Ye Tian understood.
Next, Wolf Bone Saint Beast and Violent Ape Saint Beast revealed another secret, which was the purpose of those foreign forces' frantic desire to invade other realms.
All along, Ye Tian thought the reason those foreign forces invaded was for resources and to comprehend foreign rules to break through to the level of Supreme Ancestor, Supreme Saint Beast, or Bone Emperor, but that was only part of the reason. The more important reason was for the Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals!

Chapter 1504: The Great Calamity Has Arrived!

Chapter 1504: The Great Calamity Has Arrived!

When the Wolf Bone Saint Beast and the Violent Ape Saint Beast mentioned the Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, Ye Tian asked curiously, "What exactly are Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, and what use do they have?"
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast explained, "Origin Rule Calamity Crystals are treasures that are only born during a Great Calamity of Heaven and Earth. They are extremely rare and precious. They can help a top-tier Saint Beast comprehend the rules of a world much faster. Otherwise, we could only stay in a foreign world for a very short time. How could we possibly create Saint Arts that are compatible with a foreign world? There simply wouldn't be enough time. Only by obtaining an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal is there hope of becoming an Ultimate Saint Beast..."
At this point, he cast a curious glance at the Heyuan Saint Beast, showing a look of wonder, and the Violent Ape Saint Beast looked curious as well.
If Ye Tian didn't know about the Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, how did he break through to become an Ultimate Saint Beast?
Previously, the two of them had assumed that Ye Tian had been lucky enough to obtain an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal during the last Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain, and had spent those long ages secretly comprehending the rules of the Dark Forbidden Domain to create compatible Saint Arts, thus allowing him to break through to the Ultimate Saint Beast realm.
But looking at it now, that didn't seem to be the case.
For a moment, they were extremely curious.
Ye Tian also knew that Wolf Bone and the others were suspicious, but he didn't care.
This clone of his was also at the Ultimate Saint Beast realm; he didn't fear Wolf Bone and the others, and they wouldn't make a move against him because of this.
At this moment.
Ye Tian finally understood how foreign experts achieved their breakthroughs. Foreign experts didn't have special duplicated bodies like he did, which allowed him to infiltrate foreign lands and constantly comprehend their rules.
They could only infiltrate a foreign world to comprehend its rules during a Great Calamity, but the duration of a calamity wouldn't be very long. In such a short time, no matter how monstrous one's talent was, it was impossible to fully comprehend foreign rules!
And once they left the foreign world and returned to their own, there would be no hope of creating Saint Arts or Progenitor Arts compatible with that foreign world.
However, if one obtained an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, they could continue to comprehend the rules of that foreign world even after leaving it.
"So you're saying that if one obtains a foreign Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, even without entering that foreign world, there's hope of becoming an Ultimate Saint Beast?"
Ye Tian asked.
"Yes!"
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast nodded.
At this point, Ye Tian felt a surge of interest in the foreign Origin Rule Calamity Crystals. If he could obtain one, he could bring it back to the Human Race for his relatives to study. Once they fully comprehended it, they could step into the Ultimate Progenitor realm.
"The foreign Origin Rule Calamity Crystals must be useful to us Ultimate Saint Beasts as well, right?"
Ye Tian asked again.
"Of course they are!" The Wolf Bone Saint Beast said with a smile. "Our goal is to become second-tier Ultimate Saint Beasts, so we must create Ultimate Saint Techniques compatible with the foreign rules, and then fuse two Ultimate Saint Techniques to break the shackles and comprehend a Paramount Saint Technique. Therefore, the foreign Origin Rule Calamity Crystals are still of immense help to us. Furthermore, they can greatly increase our cultivation. As long as we don't completely refine the crystal, it can slowly recover. Thus, a single foreign Origin Rule Calamity Crystal is enough to make even Ultimate Saint Beasts fight to the death. Normally, the number of crystals born during a calamity is uncertain; there might only be a few, or there might be dozens. There is evidence suggesting that the more slaughter there is, the more crystals will eventually be born."
"The more slaughter, the more Origin Rule Calamity Crystals?" Ye Tian frowned, realizing what this implied. "So, is this why those foreign forces slaughter so frenziedly and destroy everything during every calamity?"
"Yes!"
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast nodded and then said, "Aside from our three Great Saint Sects, other forces simply cannot survive. After the calamity, I'm afraid only the territories of our three Great Holy Lands will still have living beings; other regions will likely be nearly annihilated. Only after the calamity passes will those regions slowly give birth to new life and worlds."
Ye Tian now understood completely.
In the Dark Forbidden Domain, various Dark Holy Lands were born—the Dark Destruction Domain, the Dark Saint Domain, the Dark Soul Domain... these Dark Holy Lands emerged, one for every Dark Era, with nine Dark Holy Lands born over nine Dark Eras.
But why were the Dark Holy Lands from the previous three calamities gone, with not even a trace of ruins or the worlds from before the calamities remaining?
Now, he knew. The previous Dark Holy Lands and their many worlds had all been wiped out by foreign experts.
After the calamity, the Dark Forbidden Domain became an empty world, waiting to be nurtured anew.
The Holy Region could at least preserve the three Great Saint Sects, but the Dark Forbidden Domain previously had no Ultimate Progenitors and thus couldn't protect any location. Those top-tier Progenitors were all busy trying to hide; why would they bother protecting those Dark Holy Lands!
"No wonder those ancient Progenitors aren't keen on occupying Dark Holy Lands or developing their forces. It's all in vain; even if they develop them, they'll just be wiped out by foreign experts."
Ye Tian realized suddenly.
However, this time was different. With him guarding the Dark Forbidden Domain, he could at least protect the Human Race's territory.
Ye Tian chatted with the two Ultimate Saint Beasts for a long time.
Soon, the Great Calamity of the Holy Region arrived.
Buzz buzz buzz!!!
The rules of the entire Holy Region underwent a subtle change. The world became filled with the aura of slaughter, and it no longer suppressed foreign experts.
One by one, figures emerged from the various forbidden lands across the Holy Region. The weakest among them were comparable to ordinary Progenitors.
As for those below the Progenitor level, there was no point in them coming. They couldn't even cross the distance of a single world, and they were too weak to even qualify as cannon fodder.
At the same time.
In the areas surrounding the Sea-Sky Saint Sect, countless experts gathered, seeking the protection of the sect. As for the weak, there was no way to look after them.
Countless experts traversed the various regions of the Holy Region, and endless living beings were turned to ash in an instant.
Countless resources were seized by them, becoming the energy for the foreign experts to grow stronger.
In the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Ye Tian established contact with his clone, the Heyuan Saint Beast. Knowing that the Great Calamity of the Holy Region had arrived, he split off a duplicated body.
However, it took some time to condense a duplicated body at the Ultimate Progenitor level, and it required a significant amount of energy—clearly a limitation.
Before long, this duplicated body was condensed, possessing the same combat power as the original body.
"Go!"
The duplicated body crossed over to the Sea-Sky Forbidden Land and easily slaughtered all the exotic beasts within.
He intended to pass through the gate, enter the Holy Region, and take the opportunity to occupy the Sea-Sky Saint Sect.

Chapter 1505: This Gate Belongs to the Human Race Now!

Chapter 1505: This Gate Belongs to the Human Race Now!

"Suppression?"
Ye Tian attempted to step through the gate and enter the Sanctuary World, but he felt a sense of suppression emanating from the gate.
This gate allowed top-tier Ancestors to enter easily, but Ye Tian's duplicate body had reached the level of a Supreme Ancestor, and thus was restricted by the gate.
Of course, Ye Tian could also force his way in, though it would require paying a certain price.
Whoosh!!!!!
Ye Tian brought out a massive amount of energy resources and infused them into the gate, causing it to glow brilliantly.
At the same time, Ye Tian forced his way through. He suffered the gate's backlash; even if his body was injured and his strength declined after passing through, it didn't matter.
With his current power, even with a decline in strength, he could still suppress ordinary Supreme Saint Beasts.
Boom!!!!!
Ye Tian forcibly crossed the gate and entered the Sanctuary World.
The Hai Tian Saint Sect was currently preparing for the Great Calamity. Although many Saint Beasts guarded the gate, the two Supreme Saint Beasts were not present.
Upon arriving in the Sanctuary World, Ye Tian instantly slaughtered these Saint Beasts and a large number of ordinary Hai Tian Saint Sect disciples. Even top-tier Saint Beasts could not withstand a single blow from him.
Toward these exotic beasts and creatures of a foreign realm, Ye Tian felt no pity.
The Dark Forbidden Domain had faced three Great Calamities, and in each one, the creatures of the domain were wiped out by foreign worlds, with only a few top-tier Ancestors surviving. Why should he feel pity for other foreign worlds? Even if all the living beings in the Sanctuary World were wiped out, it would be of little consequence.
The headquarters of the Hai Tian Saint Sect was not far from the gate. At this moment, the Wolf Bone Saint Beast and the Violent Ape Saint Beast became aware of Ye Tian's arrival, feeling both shocked and bewildered.
They didn't know much about the Dark Forbidden Domain of this era, but they were well aware that there should absolutely be no Supreme Ancestors in the Dark Forbidden Domain right now. After all, those beings couldn't travel to other foreign worlds, nor did they possess the Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals of other worlds. How could they possibly break through to the Supreme Ancestor realm?
Yet now, a Supreme Ancestor had actually come from the Dark Forbidden Domain?
"Kill him! This gate must not be lost. With the Great Calamity approaching, we cannot let a Supreme Ancestor from the Dark Forbidden Domain destroy everything we have!"
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast and the Violent Ape Saint Beast thought to themselves.
They believed that with the three Supreme Saint Beasts of the Hai Tian Saint Sect working together, there was a great chance they could slay a Supreme Ancestor who had just crossed the gate and was in a weakened state.
"He Yuan Saint Beast, let us strike together and kill this Supreme Ancestor!"
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast sent a telepathic message.
Boom!!!!
The three Supreme Saint Beasts instantly charged from the Hai Tian Saint Sect headquarters toward Ye Tian.
Meanwhile, the other Saint Beasts retreated one after another. They could not interfere in a battle at the level of Supreme Saint Beasts and Supreme Ancestors; even the shockwaves alone could claim their lives.
Right at that moment, the He Yuan Saint Beast changed his line of attack and struck the weakest one, the Wolf Bone Saint Beast.
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast never expected the He Yuan Saint Beast to attack him, so he had no defenses prepared.
Instantly, the Wolf Bone Saint Beast was sent flying by the blow, suffering significant injuries.
And at that moment, Ye Tian's attack arrived.
Ye Tian did not hold back at all, unleashing an attack at the second tier of the Supreme Ancestor level. Although his strength had been weakened by the gate's backlash, his offensive power still reached the second tier.
"Supreme Ancestral Technique: Tyrant Force!"
This blow landed squarely on the Wolf Bone Saint Beast.
In an instant, the Wolf Bone Saint Beast was blown apart. Although he managed to reform his body, the wounds on his form continued to crack and could not heal at all.
At this moment, he was incomparably heavily injured.
"Second tier of the Supreme Ancestor level!"
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast was dazed.
In the entire Sanctuary World, there was only one Supreme Saint Beast who had reached the second tier. The Dark Forbidden Domain hadn't even had a single Supreme Ancestor before, yet now a second-tier Supreme Ancestor had suddenly appeared. This was too surreal.
"Violent Ape Saint Beast, run!"
The Wolf Bone Saint Beast shouted.
He knew he couldn't escape. Being heavily injured, neither Ye Tian nor the He Yuan Saint Beast would let him go.
On the other hand, the Violent Ape Saint Beast still had a hope of escaping.
The Violent Ape Saint Beast knew deep down that he was no match for Ye Tian, so he didn't dare stay. He immediately began to flee, while the Wolf Bone Saint Beast risked his life to stall Ye Tian.
In the end, the Violent Ape Saint Beast managed to escape, while the Wolf Bone Saint Beast was killed by Ye Tian.
Ye Tian didn't care in the slightest about the Violent Ape Saint Beast's escape.
He wasn't a third-tier Supreme Ancestor; otherwise, he could have easily killed both Supreme Saint Beasts.
Next, Ye Tian had the He Yuan Saint Beast take over the management of the Hai Tian Saint Sect. Naturally, there were many who resisted.
But Ye Tian showed no mercy. Whoever resisted was killed instantly.
In a short amount of time, nearly half of the Saint Beasts in the Hai Tian Saint Sect were slaughtered. Some fled, while only a few remained to pledge loyalty to the He Yuan Saint Beast. As for the beasts below the Saint level, most of them surrendered. They didn't dare resist, and with the Great Calamity arriving, they couldn't survive outside. They had to rely on a Supreme Saint Beast to have any hope of living, so naturally, they didn't dare rebel.
In this way, Ye Tian had effectively taken control of the Hai Tian Saint Sect.
...
In the Sanctuary World, in a silent stretch of void.
The Violent Ape Saint Beast struck the void in fury, roaring madly.
"He Yuan Saint Beast, WHY????"
He could not understand why the He Yuan Saint Beast would help a Supreme Ancestor from the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Even if the He Yuan Saint Beast had some deal with the people of the Dark Forbidden Domain, would he have turned against his own kind?
Even if that Supreme Ancestor was powerful, if the three of them had joined forces, they might have been able to barely contend with him. They wouldn't have ended up in such a state.
"Damn that He Yuan Saint Beast! Even if you side with the Supreme Ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain, they won't value you. They might even kill you one day! Why are you so foolish?! They are an alien race—why are you of one mind with them?"
The Violent Ape Saint Beast couldn't understand, nor could he find a way to make sense of it.
However, he had no idea that the He Yuan Saint Beast was actually Ye Tian's clone. It was essentially Ye Tian himself. Helping oneself was, of course, perfectly normal.
At the Hai Tian Saint Sect.
Ye Tian began to draw upon the power of the gate to create a forbidden zone within the Sanctuary World, preparing for the future entry of the human race's Ancestors.
Previously, Ye Tian didn't know how to construct a gate, nor did he know how to build a forbidden zone.
But once the He Yuan Saint Beast became a Supreme Saint Beast, Wolf Bone and the others had informed him. Combined with the construction methods plundered from the Wolf Bone Saint Beast—and confirming nothing was hidden—he now set out to build a forbidden zone base.
A so-called forbidden zone base involved drawing power from the gate to alter the rules of an area, turning it into a forbidden land. As long as the gate wasn't destroyed, the forbidden zone would not dissipate.
Ye Tian could also build a gate himself, but the cost was too high. He would have to capture a phantom gate of a world and fuse it with countless materials to create an eternal gate.
One phantom gate is born every Dark Era; nine gates are born over nine Dark Eras.
Previously, the Dark Forbidden Domain had also birthed phantom gates, but he didn't know the construction methods then, so he hadn't occupied them.
Additionally, which foreign world a gate connects to is normally uncontrollable. Only by locking onto the coordinates of a specific foreign world can a gate be temporarily modified to connect to a designated realm.
That would be extremely troublesome.
Right now, Ye Tian didn't have time to wait. He could only utilize this gate of the Hai Tian Saint Sect.
In short, this gate now belonged to him—it belonged to the human race!.

Chapter 1506: Resource Scramble!

Chapter 1506: Resource Scramble!

Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect.
This was the most powerful of the three major holy sects in the Holy Domain World. It possessed five Supreme Holy Beasts, one of whom had reached the second level of the Supreme Holy Beast realm. There were even more Holy Beasts below the Supreme level, numbering several times more than those of the Sea-Sky Holy Sect.
Furthermore, the Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect occupied the region with the most abundant resources in the Holy Domain World.
Currently, the experts from the outworlds had not yet moved to occupy the territory of the Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect. This was a form of tacit understanding, or even a kind of cooperation; they would first wipe out the territories of smaller factions.
It could be said that during the early or middle stages of the Great Tribulation, the three major holy sects faced almost no danger.
At this time, although the Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect was preparing for war, the overall atmosphere remained peaceful.
On this day.
The Violent Ape Holy Beast arrived at the Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect and was immediately sensed by the sect's Supreme Holy Beasts.
"Violent Ape, what are you doing here?"
Voices enveloped the Violent Ape Holy Beast from all directions.
The Violent Ape Holy Beast immediately pleaded, "Wan Yuan Holy Beast, the Gate of our Sea-Sky Holy Sect has been occupied by a Supreme Ancestor from the Dark Forbidden Domain. The opponent entered through the Gate and, in cooperation with our sect's He Yuan Holy Beast, killed the Wolf Bone Holy Beast. Now, the Sea-Sky Holy Sect has fallen into his hands. That Ancestor has reached the second level of the Supreme Ancestor realm. While he hasn't yet fully established his foundation, I ask the Wan Yuan Holy Beast to help me drive him away. Otherwise, if he establishes a Forbidden Land in our Holy Domain World, we will be in deep trouble!"
Swish!
Figures emerged one after another, all of them massive exotic beasts. They were the Supreme Holy Beasts of the Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect.
One of them had six eyes and was covered in black scales.
This was the Wan Yuan Holy Beast.
"Violent Ape, you are truly useless, letting someone seize even your Gate. But right now, we cannot help you. A second-level Supreme Ancestor plus a Supreme Holy Beast is a very powerful force. If we go to war with them, what if outworld experts invade our Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect? We cannot take such a risk for your Sea-Sky Holy Sect. After the Great Tribulation, the opponent must leave. At that time, we will help you kill He Yuan Holy Beast and reclaim the Sea-Sky Holy Sect."
Wan Yuan Holy Beast suggested.
"Fine!"
The Violent Ape Holy Beast agreed helplessly.
Without the help of the Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect, he could not kill He Yuan Holy Beast on his own.
In the days that followed, the Violent Ape Holy Beast stayed within the Ten Thousand Beasts Holy Sect.
...
After Ye Tian occupied the Sea-Sky Forbidden Land, he dispatched a large number of humans to renovate it. Even the various Ancestors of the human race were sent to guard the Sea-Sky Forbidden Land.
One of Ye Tian's avatars also stayed near the Sea-Sky Forbidden Land. If any top-tier Ancestors from the Dark Forbidden Domain came to invade, he would naturally be able to take action immediately.
Subsequently, a human Ancestor frequently entered and exited the Gate, bringing back vast amounts of resources from the Sea-Sky Holy Sect.
The total amount of resources possessed by the Sea-Sky Holy Sect was beyond the human race's imagination.
The human race had only existed for a few Dark Eras, while the Sea-Sky Holy Sect had existed for several Great Tribulation cycles. They had even invaded the Dark Forbidden Domain before, and the resources in their treasury were an astronomical figure.
Moreover, the Sea-Sky Holy Sect's territory was vast, with many resource-rich lands. Ye Tian now sent people to mine them extensively, transporting everything back to the human race.
After all, once the late stage of the Great Tribulation arrived, the Sea-Sky Holy Sect might not be able to be held. He naturally wanted to bring the resources back to the human race.
At the same time, the many Holy Arts and other cultivation techniques and secret methods owned by the Sea-Sky Holy Sect were also brought back to the human race, almost turning the Sea-Sky Holy Sect into an empty shell.
The duration of the Great Tribulation was not long, lasting a total of one Domain Year.
In the first hundred billion years, outworld forces would not invade the three major holy sects. Thus, Ye Tian took this opportunity to aggressively seize resources from other factions, naturally doing so under the identity of an outworld expert.
Consequently, Ye Tian's duplicated body personally took action, crossing one territory after another to seize the resources of many factions. If anyone resisted, he would kill them directly.
Countless resources and countless ancient texts all fell into Ye Tian's hands.
During this period, he also encountered some outworld experts. Everyone maintained a tacit understanding and did not fight, as now was not the time for conflict.
The entire Holy Domain World was filled with wailing, allowing Ye Tian to witness the horror of the Great Tribulation.
This was only the Holy Domain World; because it possessed several Supreme Holy Beasts, it could still preserve some territory. If it were the Dark Forbidden Domain, the past was even more terrifying, with everything being wiped out directly.
Year after year passed. By the later stages, basically all the relatively large factions had been annihilated, and the resources of the Holy Domain World began to grow scarce.
Even so, Ye Tian did not waste any resources. Even those useless to him were collected; at the very least, they could be used to nurture experts of the human race.
Gradually, a hundred billion years passed.
A hundred billion years was indeed not long, but it marked the transition into the middle stage of the Great Tribulation.
At this time, it was highly likely that Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals would be born in the Holy Domain World.
As for where the Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals would appear, it was hard to say; it depended on luck.
Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals would be born within a short period, and because the Holy Domain World was so vast, even those with weak cultivation might obtain one, while powerful Supreme Holy Beast-level experts might not obtain a single one.
Of course, once an Origin Rule Tribulation Crystal was obtained, unless no one saw it, the news would leak, and the possessor would be hunted by a large number of experts. Without sufficient strength, it was very difficult to keep the crystal.
On this day.
News arrived that a top-tier Holy Beast rogue cultivator in the Holy Domain World had obtained an Origin Rule Tribulation Crystal and was currently being pursued.
-------------------
In a silent void filled with the scent of blood.
A top-tier Holy Beast resembling a minotaur was hiding inside a small world, completely concealing its aura and diving deep beneath the rocky earth of the small world.
Normally, hiding like this would make it very difficult to be discovered.
However, this was the Great Tribulation.
BOOM!!!!
An outworld expert comparable to a Supreme Holy Beast arrived here. Seeing this solitary cluster of small worlds, he struck out with a wave of his hand. Countless small worlds were shattered, and this stretch of space-time was pulverized. Many hidden spaces also vanished into nothingness.
Naturally, the countless living beings inside were annihilated.
Under such an attack, that top-tier Holy Beast could no longer hide and was exposed.
"Hahaha, I didn't expect you to be hiding here. You can't run now!"
The outworld expert said excitedly.
CRACK!!!!
The top-tier Holy Beast was heavily injured by a single strike from the opponent, and the Innate Holy Artifact on its body was directly shattered.
After the second strike, this top-tier Holy Beast was killed.
Just as he was about to collect the corpse of the top-tier Holy Beast, another outworld expert appeared.
Instantly, a battle between outworld experts broke out.

Chapter 1507: The Ambition of the Blood Mist Alliance!

Chapter 1507: The Ambition of the Blood Mist Alliance!

How precious were the Origin Rule Calamity Crystals? Not only were they useful to Ultimate Ancestors, but they could even create one.
Therefore, once foreign experts heard news of an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, they would naturally fight for it at any cost.
At this moment.
Ye Tian also received the news. With a single thought, he traversed time and space to arrive at the scene.
By the time he arrived, several Ultimate-level foreign experts had already descended.
Currently, several Ultimate-level foreign experts were besieging one individual, who had clearly seized the corpse of a top-tier Sacred Beast.
Under the siege of multiple Ultimate-level foreign experts, this individual was heavily wounded.
However, at that moment, two more Ultimate-level foreign experts arrived. One of them had even reached the second tier of the Ultimate level. Together, the three Ultimate-level foreign experts fended off the siege from the others.
"A step too late!"
Ye Tian shook his head.
His strength was roughly equal to that of the second-tier Ultimate-level foreign expert, so he had no way to kill them or seize their Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
Soon, the three foreign experts fled. The others did not pursue them, knowing there was little hope. Unless two or more third-tier experts intervened, there was no chance of stopping them; otherwise, they would surely escape back to their base in a short time and send the Origin Rule Calamity Crystal back to their own foreign world.
Ye Tian wasn't surprised at all that he failed to snatch the first Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
His strength had not yet reached the level where he could sweep through everything, so it was normal that he couldn't seize it.
However, through this encounter, he gained a general understanding of the strength of these foreign experts.
Most Ultimate-level foreign experts were only comparable to first-tier Ultimate Ancestors. Second-tier Ultimate Ancestors were rare, accounting for only about one-tenth, and he had yet to see a single third-tier Ultimate Ancestor.
Perhaps among the many foreign worlds, third-tier Ultimate Ancestors were incredibly scarce, all working hard to break through to the Invincible Ancestor level, and wouldn't necessarily participate.
The foreign power corresponding to the only Rank 2 Gate in the Sacred Domain World might possess third-tier Ultimate Ancestors, but they might not necessarily deploy them.
Without third-tier Ultimate Ancestors, Ye Tian wasn't as worried.
His biggest fear was the appearance of an Invincible Ancestor; if that happened, he could forget about competing for even a single Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
……
Sacred Domain World, Blood Mist Forbidden Zone.
This was the forbidden zone where the only Rank 2 Gate in the Sacred Domain World was located, established by the foreign power known as the Blood Mist Alliance.
The Blood Mist Alliance was not actually a single organization but a coalition of multiple forces. Strictly speaking, it was formed by several powers from the Blood Mist World specifically to invade other foreign worlds.
Such an alliance was actually very difficult to form. For instance, in the Sacred Domain World, the three Great Sacred Sects would not unite; after all, they could each open their own Gates to plunder resources from other foreign worlds, so there was no need to join forces.
After all, experts who reached the level of Ultimate Ancestor were extremely proud and would not easily unite.
But the Blood Mist Alliance had united, combining the power of an entire world. Naturally, there was a truly powerful figure suppressing them, which made them very cohesive. Otherwise, they would have long since schemed against each other during missions, leading to the alliance's collapse.
The Blood Mist Alliance was terrifying, which was why the three Great Sacred Sects of the Sacred Domain World and other foreign powers would generally unite to oppose them.
Otherwise, the Blood Mist Alliance would have long ago wiped out the three Great Sacred Sects and the bases of other foreign powers, seizing all the Origin Rule Calamity Crystals for themselves.
Yet this time, the Blood Mist Alliance had not dispatched many foreign experts. For example, they hadn't paid much attention to the competition for the first Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
If anyone were to come here, they would find that many Ultimate-level foreign experts had gathered.
Within the blood-colored mist, figures sat upon thrones. There were about dozens of them, all at the Ultimate Ancestor level, with no shortage of second-tier experts among them.

Suddenly.
Boom!!!!
A terrifying figure emerged, clearly surpassing the second tier and reaching the third tier, infinitely close to the level of an Invincible Ancestor.
"Greetings, Lord Baigui!"
"Greetings, Lord Baigui!"
"Greetings, Lord Baigui!"
One by one, the foreign experts stood up and bowed respectfully.
True Emperor Baigui, one of the three Vice Alliance Leaders of the Blood Mist Alliance, a third-tier Ultimate True Emperor.
"True Emperor" corresponded to the Ancestor level; it was their title for it.
An Ultimate True Emperor was an Ultimate Ancestor; only the name was different, while the path was similar.
True Emperor Baigui looked at the many True Emperors and spoke: "Our Blood Mist Alliance has completely digested another foreign world and destroyed all Gates not belonging to the alliance, gaining 100% control over that world. Now, our Blood Mist Alliance has sufficient strength to invade the Sacred Domain World. This Sacred Domain World has already passed its 'newbie period.' Unlike some newborn foreign worlds where we cannot completely transform them due to the protection of rules, the Sacred Domain World does not have this issue. Once we gain complete control here, we can begin the transformation to make this world adapt to our Blood Mist Alliance. At that time, our Blood Mist Alliance will have one more foreign world."
"Lord Baigui, when do we strike?" an Ultimate True Emperor asked.
"Wait a bit longer. During the late stages of the Great Calamity, when the source of the Sacred Domain World is weak, it will be easier for us to attempt the transformation. Furthermore, let them slaughter more living beings to clear out the Sacred Domain World for us; there's no rush to act. None of these forces have third-tier Ultimate True Emperors; once I take action, they won't be able to stop me at all. Moreover, in a while, another third-tier Ultimate True Emperor will arrive. With two third-tier Ultimate True Emperors combined with over ten second-tier Ultimate True Emperors, no force will be able to contend with us!" True Emperor Baigui said.
"Yes!"
The many True Emperors responded one by one.
At this time, the other foreign powers and the native Ultimate Sacred Beasts of the Sacred Domain World were not necessarily aware of the Blood Mist Alliance's ambitions and were still searching for Origin Rule Calamity Crystals.
Ye Tian was also unaware of the Blood Mist Alliance's plans, but even if he knew, he wouldn't be worried.
After all, no matter how bad the situation got, the Blood Mist Alliance currently had no way to invade the Dark Forbidden Zone.
Besides, given his rate of progress, by the time the Great Calamity hit the Dark Forbidden Zone, he might have already advanced to the third tier of the Ultimate Ancestor level and wouldn't fear the Blood Mist Alliance at all.
In the blink of an eye, another few billion years passed, and the second Origin Rule Calamity Crystal appeared.

Chapter 1508: The Blood Mist Alliance Strikes!

Chapter 1508: The Blood Mist Alliance Strikes!

When the second Origin Rule Calamity Crystal appeared, Ye Tian received the news relatively early. Thus, he arrived at the scene immediately, heavily injured three Supreme Ancestors, and ultimately snatched this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
After seizing this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, Ye Tian returned to the Sea Sky Holy Sect to observe it.
"So this is an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal!"
Ye Tian carefully sensed the rules upon it. They indeed belonged to the rules of the Sanctuary World, and they were the most fundamental origin rules. Comprehending an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal was naturally better and faster than cultivating within the Sanctuary World itself, and the crystal contained powerful origin power.
Ye Tian could sense that if he refined this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, it would be enough to raise his cultivation level slightly and even temper his Supreme Ancestor Body.
However, compared to the benefits brought by creating a Supreme Ancestral Technique, a mere Origin Rule Calamity Crystal was nothing.
Yet, not just anyone could create a Supreme Ancestral Technique.
For instance, in the Sanctuary World, over such a long period of time, there had only been one second-tier Supreme Holy Beast.
"It is more cost-effective to use this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal in the future to comprehend and create a Supreme Ancestral Technique or to give it to the Human Race!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Consequently, he sent the Origin Rule Calamity Crystal back to the Dark Forbidden Zone. Through the hands of a Human Ancestor, it passed through the door and was delivered to his main body.
Following that, every so often, an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal would be born within the Sanctuary World.
However, his luck was poor afterward, and the subsequent Origin Rule Calamity Crystals were all snatched away by other Ancestors.
As time passed, a total of nearly thirty Origin Rule Calamity Crystals were born in the Sanctuary World.
"I only managed to snatch two!"
Ye Tian sighed.
He also wanted to seize more Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, but once other Ancestors obtained one, they could return to their respective foreign worlds at the fastest possible speed. He had no way to pursue them.
After all, the other foreign worlds had not yet reached the time of their Great Calamity. If he pursued them there, he would be directly obliterated by the foreign world's power.
Unless he was willing to copy the body of a powerhouse from that foreign world to give chase, but that would expose his ability, so it wasn't worth it.
Nevertheless, among so many Supreme Ancestors, being able to snatch two Origin Rule Calamity Crystals was already quite good.
He did not keep either of these two Origin Rule Calamity Crystals for himself; he sent them both back to his human main body.
At this time, the Great Calamity of the Sanctuary World had reached its late stages. Except for the territories of the three Great Holy Sects, all other regions had become a void. Not a single resource remained; everything had been plundered. Countless worlds had been reduced to fragments, and the living beings within them had naturally all perished.
Myriad Beasts Holy Sect.
Wan Yuan Holy Beast was somewhat flustered at this moment because this Great Calamity was far too different from those in the past.
In the past, the True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance would collect resources on a large scale and would even be attacking the three Great Holy Sects by now. The three Great Holy Sects would have to unite with other foreign worlds to keep the Blood Mist Alliance in check.
But now, the Blood Mist Alliance had hardly made a move. Even for collecting resources, they had only dispatched a few Supreme True Emperors. This was not the style of the Blood Mist Alliance.
Furthermore, through investigation, the Blood Mist Forbidden Land of the Blood Mist Alliance had been shrouded. Even Supreme-level powerhouses could not peer inside, and no one knew what they were doing.
Under such circumstances, all Supreme-level foreign powerhouses knew the Blood Mist Alliance had some issues, but the other foreign powerhouses weren't worried. Their bases were not in the Sanctuary World; at worst, they could just withdraw. They weren't afraid of the Blood Mist Alliance at all.
But the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect was afraid!
The Sanctuary World was the very foundation of the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect. They couldn't just run away.
"I hope the Blood Mist Alliance just has problems at their headquarters and lacks the strength to participate in this calamity, rather than it being some kind of conspiracy!"
Wan Yuan Holy Beast thought secretly.
However, not long after, a Holy Beast from the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect sent word that a large number of True Emperors from the Blood Mist Alliance were attacking, including many Supreme True Emperors.
Shortly after the message arrived, that Holy Beast went silent. Clearly, they had been discovered and obliterated by the True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance.
……
One of the three Great Holy Sects of the Sanctuary World, the Gilded Holy Sect.
This sect was even stronger than the Sea Sky Holy Sect, possessing three Supreme Holy Beasts, and its other Holy Beasts were far more numerous than those of the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
But suddenly, many True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance arrived here. It was all too abrupt, leaving the Gilded Holy Sect no time to react.
Hum!!!!
Countless rays of light swept across the region occupied by the Gilded Holy Sect. Countless worlds were annihilated, and countless beings perished. Even many Holy Beasts had no power to resist and were instantly killed.
·········Asking for flowers··· ·····
If the Ancestors in the Dark Forbidden Zone saw this scene, they would likely fall into despair.
After all, Holy Beasts with combat power comparable to Ancestors had become like ants at this moment.
"Blood Mist Alliance, you've gone too far!!!!!"
The three Supreme Holy Beasts of the Gilded Holy Sect shouted in rage.
They didn't think about fighting to the death with the Blood Mist Alliance because they knew they couldn't win. Instead, they tried their best to break through the encirclement to unite with the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect and then with other foreign forces to contend with the Blood Mist Alliance.
However, a giant hand reached across time and space, instantly grabbing one of the Supreme Holy Beasts.
With a gentle squeeze, that Supreme Holy Beast was crushed.
Of course, this Supreme Holy Beast still hadn't perished, but before he could fully heal and recover, another strike landed. This time, every trace of the Supreme Holy Beast's life was completely wiped out, erased entirely from the world.
... .. 0
There was no power to resist!
"A third-tier Supreme True Emperor!!!"
The other two surviving Supreme Holy Beasts cried out in despair.
They had never seen such a powerhouse; in the past, the Blood Mist Alliance had never dispatched such an expert!
Why would such a powerhouse appear in the late stages of the Great Calamity? This wasn't normal!
However, they couldn't escape either.
Soon, they also died at the hands of that third-tier Supreme True Emperor of the Blood Mist Alliance—the White Turtle True Emperor.
The destruction of the Gilded Holy Sect naturally reached the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect and the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
Immediately, Ye Tian had all the human powerhouses withdraw from the Sea Sky Forbidden Land. Then, Ye Tian's copied body, taking his clone He Yuan Holy Beast, evacuated the Sea Sky Holy Sect at once. He abandoned the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
He knew very well that since the Blood Mist Alliance had wiped out the Gilded Holy Sect in an instant, their next target would likely be the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
He had no way to contend with the Blood Mist Alliance, so he didn't want to lose his clone or his copied body.
The powerhouses of the Blood Mist Alliance could enter the Sea Sky Forbidden Land through the door, so the humans naturally couldn't stay to guard it. They had to evacuate to avoid losses.
It must be said that Ye Tian's decision was very clear.
Soon, the Blood Mist Alliance arrived at the Sea Sky Holy Sect and destroyed it with a wave of a hand.
And at this time, Ye Tian arrived at the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect and.
