Chapter 1545: Occupying the Holy Region World!

Chapter 1545: Occupying the Holy Region World!

The weakest of the Calamity Beasts Ye Tian hunted were over a hundred-calamity level, making their value much higher than the sixty-calamity beasts he had hunted before.
A sixty-calamity beast was worth at least thirty thousand contribution points, while a beast of over a hundred calamities was worth at least a hundred thousand points.
The thirteen Calamity Beasts Ye Tian hunted were ultimately exchanged for 2.01 million contribution points. Since he hadn't spent much time doing so, his speed of accumulating contribution points was incredibly fast. If the other Invincibles of the Heavenly Wind Sea knew of this, they would likely be driven mad with envy.
With so many contribution points, Ye Tian not only lacked no resources, but he could also spend a long time at Nine Yang Mountain to comprehend the Nine Yang Fish.
As time passed, Ye Tian comprehended various Eternal Rules, slowly refining them as his mastery over the different Eternal Rules continued to improve.
Additionally, Ye Tian used his contribution points to purchase various treasures that could enhance his cultivation, among which top-grade Calamity Stones could also be used for that purpose.
As for the top-tier Invincible Calamity Body technique, "Ten Thousand Origins Returning to Ruins," Ye Tian's progress was not fast. This was because he frequently encountered flaws or dangers, requiring him to perfect it time and again to ensure it was perfectly compatible with himself before allowing his main body to practice it.
Consequently, his cultivation speed in this regard was much slower.
However, compared to others, Ye Tian's cultivation speed was already countless times faster.
One domain epoch after another passed. Unknowingly, Ye Tian's current seclusion had exceeded the duration of one Dark Era.
Ye Tian's contribution points had not decreased; instead, they grew more numerous. From the initial two million-plus points, they had reached over ten million points, and most of them remained unused, as he had only spent a small fraction.
In terms of strength, Ye Tian's progress was immense.
"The Ten Thousand Origins Returning to Ruins has finally reached minor success! My cultivation has also increased significantly compared to the past, equivalent to the late stage of a Fifth-tier Invincible!" Ye Tian said happily.
As for Invincible Ancestral Techniques, he could have easily created several, but he was in no hurry.
If he raised his cultivation to the point where it was difficult to improve further and brought his Invincible Calamity Body to the second stage of perfection, he could then create several Invincible Ancestral Techniques to step into the Fourth-tier Invincible realm, maximizing the benefits he would receive.
Although he hadn't continued creating Invincible Ancestral Techniques, his insights into them were not low. Many techniques were only one step away from being created, but he held back. Once his cultivation and Calamity Body reached their peak, he could immediately bring those unformed Invincible Ancestral Techniques to life.
This was his plan.
……
Dark Forbidden Zone.
The human race had already become the sole race of the Dark Forbidden Zone. Other races could no longer survive and had all perished. Furthermore, the humans occupied the vast majority of the Dark Forbidden Zone, abandoning only a few areas that were truly devoid of resources.
As time passed, the human population became too large, leading to the Dark Forbidden Zone becoming somewhat insufficient. If they forced themselves to stay within its confines, internal conflict would become inevitable.
Therefore, occupying other foreign worlds and transforming them to be suitable for human life was currently an urgent task for the human race.
In fact, any Super-Famous power would take this step; for instance, the Blood Mist Alliance had done the same in the past.
Additionally, powers like Calamity Black Mountain and the Firmament Sword Tomb also possessed more than one foreign world; they had several, all under their control.
As a member of the Heavenly Wind Sea, Ye Tian naturally knew how to transform foreign worlds, so he prepared to take action against one.
"I'll choose the Holy Region World!"
Ye Tian decided.
On this day.
The Great Calamity of the Holy Region World arrived. Ye Tian led a group of human Ancestors and a few Supreme Ancestors as they descended upon the Holy Region World.
The human race now had quite a few Supreme Ancestors. After all, Ye Tian could exchange for many treasures from the Heavenly Wind Sea, some of which helped Ancestors break through to the Supreme Ancestor level. Thus, the number of human Supreme Ancestors was constantly increasing and had already reached several dozen.
After Ye Tian descended upon the Holy Region World, he immediately set about wiping out its local powers.
In a short time, the forces of the Holy Region World were completely eradicated. Even those foreign powers could not withstand the human race; their gates were destroyed one by one, and they abandoned the Holy Region World, leaving only the Super-Famous power, the Blood Mist Alliance.
------------------------
Blood Mist World.
The high-level members of the Blood Mist Alliance were holding a meeting.
The several vice-leaders of the Blood Mist Alliance were not qualified to attend this meeting. Those eligible were the Alliance Leader and the three Grand Elders. The three Grand Elders almost never interfered with the alliance's internal affairs, spending most of their time cultivating in the Tianlin Realm.
But this time, all three Grand Elders had returned.
The Blood Mist Alliance Leader, Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor, spoke: "Three Grand Elders, the Holy Region World was originally one of the worlds we planned to occupy, but unexpectedly, our previous plan failed. Now, a human power is opposing us, and this time they have gone too far, actually wanting to seize the Holy Region World as well, even killing some of our Supreme experts."
"What is the opponent's strength?" asked Mingli Mist Ancestor, one of the three Grand Elders.
"There aren't many Supreme experts, and almost all of them are at the first level. We haven't seen any third-level Invincibles. The truly powerful one is the human leader, the Myriad Law Ancestor, who should be an Invincible," Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor said.
An Invincible!
The three Grand Elders frowned, finding the situation somewhat difficult.
Although the Blood Mist Alliance had a total of four Invincibles, and Mingli Mist Ancestor was even a Fifth-tier Invincible, Invincibles varied in strength, and a Fifth-tier Invincible wasn't considered particularly high.
Moreover, it was just one Holy Region World; it wasn't an exceptionally precious asset. At worst, they could just switch to another foreign world.
At this moment, Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor added: "According to our information, our alliance's Supreme experts once fought that Myriad Law Ancestor. At that time, he was still in the Supreme realm. He hasn't been an Invincible for long; he's a newly ascended Invincible. If we let this go, it would be equivalent to our Blood Mist Alliance backing down. We absolutely cannot let it go!"
The three Grand Elders agreed; they definitely couldn't let it go.
If the opponent were an ancient Invincible, they shouldn't provoke him, but a newly ascended Invincible was definitely not that strong. No matter how monstrous one's talent, it still took time to grow!
Therefore, the Blood Mist Alliance could easily kill a newly ascended Invincible.
However, Mingli Mist Ancestor then said: "This time, the three of you will take action. I cannot go. You should be very clear that in one of the foreign worlds we occupy, that specific item is about to appear. I must stay there at all times; I cannot lose the greater for the smaller!"
"Understood!"
Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor and the others nodded one after another.

Chapter 1546: Slaying Three Invincible Ones!

Chapter 1546: Slaying Three Invincible Ones!

Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor and the others were well aware that the Ancestor of Myriad Laws occupying a foreign realm and provoking the Blood Mist Alliance was far less important than the truly major matter facing the alliance.
That matter was enough to change the destiny of the Blood Mist Alliance and was the most urgent priority at hand.
The Sacred Realm.
Ye Tian had cleared the entire Sacred Realm. Even the most deeply hidden Supreme Beings and the Sacred Beasts below that level had all been found and wiped out by him one by one.
This was a necessary step in occupying a realm. Only when the living beings of a foreign realm were completely annihilated could one easily seize the authority of that world. If many living beings or several Supreme Beings remained, it would be nearly impossible to seize authority or transform the entire Sacred Realm.
"Let the transformation begin,"
Ye Tian murmured.
Boom!!!
Under the control of secret techniques, the Second-tier Gate that Ye Tian had specifically established began to expand its base, encroaching upon the entire territory of the Sacred Realm.
Occupying a foreign realm required the use of a Gate. A Gate essentially utilized loopholes in the rules to cross between foreign realms; therefore, it could also use those loopholes to change part of a foreign realm's rules or even assimilate them.
Of course, the prerequisite was possessing the secret techniques to occupy a foreign realm's rules.
Such secret techniques were absolute secrets within foreign realms, but in an Eternal Realm like the Tianlin Realm, they were not particularly precious. The Tianfeng Sea had various such secret techniques, and they were quite cheap. Thus, Ye Tian had purchased several such techniques to handle various special situations.
At this rate, it would only take several billion years for the Second-tier Gate to completely transform the entire Sacred Realm, making the rules of this foreign realm similar to those of the Dark Forbidden Zone.
This way, the living beings of the Dark Forbidden Zone could enter the Sacred Realm to live.
Even if the Second-tier Gate were destroyed, the rules of the Sacred Realm would remain unchanged and would not revert.
Time passed slowly, and the speed at which the Sacred Realm was being transformed grew faster and faster, even far exceeding the flight speed of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.
Meanwhile, Ye Tian remained stationed near the Second-tier Gate connecting the Dark Forbidden Zone and the Sacred Realm to prevent anyone from destroying it. Once the Second-tier Gate was destroyed, all efforts would be wasted, just as had happened to the Blood Mist Alliance before.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian sensed Invincible Ones approaching, and more than one.
At first, he thought they were just Invincible Ones passing through.
After all, if an Invincible One were traveling to the Tianlin Realm, they would pass through various foreign realms. Passing through the Sacred Realm was quite normal.
As long as they didn't provoke him, he wouldn't stop these passing Invincible Ones.
But soon, he realized these Invincible Ones were not just passing through.
Three Invincible Ones descended here together and were searching for him. They quickly locked onto the location of the Second-tier Gate and his position.
"People looking for trouble?"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
He hadn't offended any Invincible Ones, so logically, no Invincible One should be coming to trouble him.
After a brief thought, he roughly guessed who these people were.
The Blood Mist Alliance!
Several Supreme Beings of the Sacred Realm had been here earlier, unwilling to leave, and had been blasted to death by him.
Therefore, it was very likely that the Blood Mist Alliance, a super-tier power, had come to find trouble with him. And since they had dispatched three Invincible Ones at once, it was clear how much importance the Blood Mist Alliance placed on him.
Rumble!!!
The three Invincible Ones descended not far from Ye Tian, their eyes fixed on him.
If an Invincible One did not take action or reveal their aura, it was difficult to know their realm and strength.
Ye Tian's speed of progress was too fast, so he had learned a secret technique to hide his aura early on. He was worried that walking through the Tianfeng Sea would attract unnecessary trouble and attention due to his rapid increase in strength. Therefore, he habitually hid his aura, only revealing the realm of an Invincible One, but it was difficult for others to know his true strength.
In the eyes of others, Ye Tian was definitely an Invincible One, but it was hard to confirm whether his aura was at the level of a Sixth-rank or Fifth-rank Invincible One.
The three Invincible Ones of the Blood Mist Alliance naturally did not believe Ye Tian was a Fifth-rank Invincible One. After all, Ye Tian had only recently broken through to the Invincible level; he was bound to be a Sixth-rank Invincible One, and a very weak one at that.
"Are you the Ancestor of Myriad Laws?"
The leader of the Blood Mist Alliance, Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor, asked coldly.
"I am the Ancestor of Myriad Laws. Are you perhaps the Invincible Ones of the Blood Mist Alliance?" Ye Tian said.
"Correct!" Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor nodded. "You actually killed the Supreme Beings of our Blood Mist Alliance; this is a provocation against us. Furthermore, you dare to occupy the Sacred Realm. This Sacred Realm was already designated as the next foreign realm for our alliance to occupy. You are seizing the territory of the Blood Mist Alliance. You are also an Invincible One, and cultivation is not easy. If you are willing to compensate our Blood Mist Alliance with one million Source Rule Calamity Crystals, then we shall let this matter go!"
One million Source Rule Calamity Crystals was nothing to a slightly wealthy Invincible One, but for a newly ascended Invincible One, it was definitely a massive sum.
Therefore, the demand from Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor and the others was incredibly excessive.
"Heh!"
Ye Tian gave a cold laugh.
A mere million Source Rule Calamity Crystals was indeed nothing to him; he could easily produce them.
But why should he give them to the Blood Mist Alliance?
"I am in a very bad mood right now. If you get lost immediately, I won't kill you. If you stay here any longer, then stay here forever!" Ye Tian threatened directly.
"Seeking death!"
The three Invincible Ones of the Blood Mist Alliance were furious and immediately attacked.
They intended to instantly kill this Invincible One. After all, the three of them had cultivated for a long time and were definitely at the top among ordinary Sixth-rank Invincible Ones, far surpassing the average.
However, they had encountered Ye Tian.
Puchi!
Ye Tian struck with his blade. The Mid-grade Calamity Tool saber slashed through the bodies of the three Invincible Ones.
In an instant, the physical bodies of the three Invincible Ones were cut in two, and a terrifying power began to erode their flesh.
In the next moment, their bodies were being annihilated and their souls were collapsing, completely unable to recover.
"No!"
Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor cried out in despair.
Then, Ye Tian struck with another slash, completely erasing their lives.
Three Invincible Ones died at Ye Tian's hands like mere ants.
----------------------
In a foreign realm controlled by the Blood Mist Alliance, Mingli Mist Ancestor was stationed there when he suddenly felt a surge of palpitations and panic.
"Could something have happened to Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor and the others? It shouldn't be possible, right?" Mingli Mist Ancestor thought.
He did not possess a communication item capable of transmitting across two foreign realms. Such items were extremely precious and not something he could own, so he had no way to contact Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor and the others.
However.
Once Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor and the others perished, some of the treasures they left at the Blood Mist Alliance headquarters would become ownerless.
Consequently, the Blood Mist Alliance soon learned that Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor had fallen, and this news was immediately relayed to Mingli Mist Ancestor.
"This is bad, we've provoked a formidable enemy!"
Mingli Mist Ancestor's pupils shrank violently.

Chapter 1547: The Secretive Yuhua World!

Chapter 1547: The Secretive Yuhua World!

In Ancestor Mingli’s view, the fall of Ancestor Blood Shadow and the others was definitely related to Ye Tian, the Ancestor of Myriad Laws. Perhaps Ye Tian hadn't acted personally, but another Invincible had.

Regardless of the circumstances, the Blood Mist Alliance had offended the Ancestor of Myriad Laws.

If the Ancestor of Myriad Laws brought fifth-grade Invincibles to invade the Blood Mist Alliance, they might discover this place.

Essentially, without a thorough investigation of this foreign world, its secrets would remain hidden. But once an invasion occurred, those secrets would surely be uncovered.

When that time came, he wouldn't be able to protect this place at all.

“I shouldn't have provoked the Ancestor of Myriad Laws!”

Ancestor Mingli said regretfully.

He had thought it would be a very simple matter—three Invincibles could easily kill an ordinary sixth-grade Invincible—but he hadn't expected it to fail.

After all, he had originally thought that if they didn't act, it would arouse suspicion from the outside world, and someone might come to investigate. It seemed better to strike first.

But now, the situation was a catastrophic mistake.

“I hope the fall of those three Invincibles from the Blood Mist Alliance was just an accident, and that the Ancestor of Myriad Laws or other Invincibles don't plan to invade the Blood Mist Alliance!” Ancestor Mingli thought to himself.

……

Ye Tian did not immediately move against the Blood Mist Alliance because the transformation of the Sacred Domain World was not yet complete; he couldn't leave at this time.

He would deal with the Blood Mist Alliance once he had handled the affairs of the Sacred Domain World.

And so, time slowly passed.

Finally, on this day, the Sacred Domain World was completely transformed. The rules here were now consistent with the rules of the Dark Forbidden Zone. Creatures from the Dark Forbidden Zone could enter without being affected in the slightest, and there were no obstacles to their cultivation.

Subsequently.

Ye Tian began a great migration of the creatures from the Dark Forbidden Zone. He even personally moved countless members of the human race to the Sacred Domain World.

The migration of the human race only truly concluded once the great tribulation of the Sacred Domain World ended.

By this time, human figures had appeared in many parts of the Sacred Domain World. It could be said that the Sacred Domain World had become the second-largest foreign world for the human race.

With this, the human race had become a super-tier power possessing two foreign worlds.

“It’s time to deal with the Blood Mist Alliance!”

Ye Tian said coldly.

The Blood Mist Alliance had dispatched three Invincibles to attack him, but he had killed them.

He wasn't sure if the Blood Mist Alliance had any more Invincibles left, but if left unchecked, they might cause trouble for the human race in the future, which was not something he wanted to see.

Therefore, he prepared to directly wipe out the Blood Mist Alliance. With his strength, he could certainly achieve this.

Soon.

Ye Tian descended upon the headquarters of the Blood Mist Alliance—the Blood Mist World.

The Blood Mist Alliance was powerful, with the number of Paragons reaching over a thousand. Among them were over a dozen Paragons in the Physical Tribulation Realm. However, these Physical Tribulation Realm Paragons almost never concerned themselves with trivial matters, focusing all their efforts on breaking through to become Invincibles.

After all, once these Physical Tribulation Realm experts reached the Invincible stage, the strength of the Blood Mist Alliance would skyrocket. Thus, becoming an Invincible was their greatest priority; everything else was minor.

However, when Ye Tian descended upon the Blood Mist Alliance, these Physical Tribulation Realm Paragons were startled.

Whoosh!

A Physical Tribulation Realm Paragon was seized by Ye Tian with one hand and interrogated directly: “How many Invincibles does your Blood Mist Alliance have?”

The Physical Tribulation Realm Paragon did not dare to hide anything and revealed: “My Lord, our Blood Mist Alliance had four Invincibles in total. Three fell not long ago, leaving only one Supreme Elder at the Invincible level. His name is Ancestor Mingli.”

“Ancestor Mingli? What is his strength?” Ye Tian asked again.

“Ancestor Mingli seems to be a fifth-grade Invincible!” the Physical Tribulation Realm Paragon replied.

“I see!”

With a surge of power, Ye Tian directly blasted the Physical Tribulation Realm expert to death.

Following that, Ye Tian began a slaughter. Countless experts comparable to Ancestors were annihilated one after another.

They wanted to flee, but no matter how they traversed time and space, they couldn't escape the Blood Mist World. Some were clever and tried to escape through the various Gates, but Ye Tian destroyed those Gates immediately, causing their plans to fail.

The Blood Mist Alliance had a total of six foreign worlds, and the one where Ancestor Mingli resided was the Yuhua World.

In the Yuhua World.

One Paragon after another arrived before Ancestor Mingli, pleading: “Ancestor Mingli, please save the headquarters! An Invincible has descended upon the Blood Mist World and quickly destroyed the Gates. We were only able to escape because we were guarding the Gates. We beg Ancestor Mingli to reinforce the headquarters and slay the enemy!”

Upon hearing this, Ancestor Mingli trembled all over.

He knew that the revenge from the Ancestor of Myriad Laws had arrived. He didn't dare to gamble; if he lost, everything would be gone.

Consequently.

Ancestor Mingli immediately destroyed the Gates connecting the Yuhua World to the other worlds, including all the second-tier Gates. In this way, the Yuhua World was no longer connected to any other foreign worlds.

Even if Ye Tian, the Ancestor of Myriad Laws, destroyed the headquarters of the Blood Mist Alliance, he wouldn't necessarily go out of his way to search for the Yuhua World. He might even assume Mingli had fled and leave it at that.

He had no other choice; he could only hope for this outcome.

In fact, he could have chosen to flee, and Ye Tian truly wouldn't have been able to find him.

However, he was reluctant to leave this place and unwilling to give up this opportunity.

After all, fifth-grade Invincible was his limit, but if he didn't abandon this fortuitous chance, he might even reach the fourth, third, or even second or first-grade Invincible realms in the future.

Therefore, he would not leave.

As time passed, the Paragons and other Fog Ancestors in the Blood Mist World were all killed by Ye Tian.

As for the endless living beings in the Blood Mist World, he didn't have the time to kill them; that would take far too long.

For Ye Tian, killing that Ancestor Mingli was the most important task.

“This Ancestor Mingli hasn't come to reinforce them. Could he have fled?”

Ye Tian thought to himself.

But a fifth-grade Invincible shouldn't be that cowardly.

Through his previous interrogations and investigations, he knew that Ancestor Mingli was in a foreign world called the Yuhua World. That world seemed to be a relatively mysterious one within the Blood Mist Alliance. Not many people from the alliance were there, and Paragons were usually not allowed to enter or leave freely; only a few Paragons stood guard there.

Furthermore, the Paragons of the Blood Mist Alliance did not have the coordinates for the Yuhua World.

Ye Tian prepared to travel to the Yuhua World through the Gates, only to find that they had been destroyed.

At this moment, Ye Tian sensed that something was wrong.

Ancestor Mingli hadn't appeared, yet the Gates were destroyed.

For an Invincible, if they wanted to flee, it would be very difficult to hunt them down. Since Invincibles could traverse various foreign worlds, they were impossible to track without special means.

If Ancestor Mingli wanted to flee, there was no need to destroy the Gates leading to the Yuhua World.

Unless the Yuhua World held a secret, and Ancestor Mingli didn't want him to know about it.

“It seems I must make a trip to the Yuhua World no matter what!”

Ye Tian thought to himself.

Chapter 1548: A Golden Mountain That Cannot Be Spied Upon!

Chapter 1548: A Golden Mountain That Cannot Be Spied Upon!

With Ye Tian's strength, finding the Yuhua World was not difficult. The Yuhua World was bound to be not very far from the Blood Mist World, so as long as he toured all the surrounding foreign worlds, he would have hope of finding it.
Thus, Ye Tian began to cross one foreign world after another.
Time passed slowly, and before he knew it, several hundred million years had gone by. During this period, Ye Tian searched many foreign worlds and conducted investigations, which took quite a bit of time.
Finally, on this day, Ye Tian descended upon a foreign world.
This foreign world had almost no living beings and was incredibly silent. However, through his understanding of the Yuhua World and an Origin Rule Tribulation Crystal of the Yuhua World obtained from within the Blood Mist Alliance...
At this moment, Ye Tian briefly contemplated the rules of this foreign world and found them to be exactly the same as that Origin Rule Tribulation Crystal.
Clearly, this was the Yuhua World.
Soon, Ye Tian found a supreme powerhouse and captured him.
"Speak, where is Ancestor Mingli Mist?"
Ye Tian said coldly.
That supreme powerhouse clearly recognized Ye Tian and couldn't help but roar, "Wanfa Ancestor, do not be so arrogant! Ancestor Mingli Mist is right here. I have already notified him; he will definitely kill you!"
In his eyes, Ancestor Mingli Mist was clearly an invincible existence who only needed to guard this place and was temporarily unable to leave, which was why Ye Tian had been able to invade the Blood Mist Alliance.
But he had no idea of Ye Tian's terror or Ancestor Mingli Mist's wariness; otherwise, how would he dare to speak like that!
...
Somewhere in the Yuhua World.
Ancestor Mingli Mist received the message from his subordinate, and his expression shifted instantly.
In reality, he had vaguely sensed an Invincible descending upon the Yuhua World, but he didn't dare to investigate for fear of attracting that Invincible's attention.
He had hoped this Invincible was just passing through, but after receiving this message, he knew who the visitor was.
Wanfa Ancestor, Ye Tian!
"Damn it, he actually found his way here!" Ancestor Mingli Mist said nervously.
He really did not want to fight Ye Tian. Although Ye Tian had killed three Invincibles of the Blood Mist Alliance, he didn't feel much anger. Compared to the opportunity in the Yuhua World, the fall of three Invincibles was nothing.
Once he obtained this opportunity and his strength rose to a fourth-grade or even third-grade Invincible, killing Ye Tian would naturally be an easy task.
But now, he didn't want any accidents to occur.
However, it seemed he could no longer hide.
An Invincible's divine sense was far from being able to probe an entire foreign world, but there were many ways to detect powerhouses within one. Unless he had an extremely powerful secret technique to hide himself, he would be unable to stay hidden.
Just then, Ye Tian took out a compass-like treasure. This was a special item purchased from the Tianfeng Sea that could detect any hidden living beings within a foreign world. Even an Invincible would find it hard to evade this compass's detection.
Buzz!!!!
The compass released a wave that covered the entire foreign world at extreme speed.
"Found him!"
Ye Tian's gaze locked onto an Invincible's position through the compass. Then, with a single thought, he pierced through time and space to look toward that infinitely distant land.
Boom!!!!
With one step across time and space, he arrived at the place where Ancestor Mingli Mist was located.
Here was a golden mountain, and upon the mountain stood a palace. Ancestor Mingli Mist was inside that palace.
"Eh, this golden mountain..."
Ye Tian was somewhat surprised.
When he had pierced through time and space to spy on this place from afar just now, he hadn't noticed this golden mountain, yet now it had appeared.
Immediately, he used his divine sense to probe the golden mountain, only to find that the space in front of him was empty. Where was any golden mountain?
"No, it's that divine sense and all forms of scrying techniques are unable to observe this golden mountain. It can only be seen with the naked eye at close range!" Ye Tian said in shock.
Once upon a time, when he was still relatively weak, he had encountered similar treasures, but that was when he was very weak.
Now, he had already reached the level of a fifth-grade Invincible, yet he still couldn't spy on this golden mountain. This showed just how precious this mountain was, or perhaps it was related to some staggering treasure to have such an effect.
At this moment, he completely understood.
Why Ancestor Mingli Mist didn't show himself, and why he wanted to destroy those gates to prevent the Yuhua World from being exposed—it was all for the opportunity here.
The opportunity here was enough to make even an Invincible go mad, willing to hide it at any cost.
"This opportunity is great, but now it's mine!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Boom!!!!
Ancestor Mingli Mist walked out of the palace, his gaze looking toward Ye Tian with complexity.
··········
"Wanfa Ancestor, I am surprised. I thought you were just a newly ascended Invincible, but I didn't expect you to already be a fifth-grade Invincible!" Ancestor Mingli Mist said indifferently.
"Ancestor Mingli Mist, what is this golden mountain?"
Ye Tian pointed at the golden mountain and asked.
"It is merely a small place of opportunity!" Ancestor Mingli Mist replied. "Wanfa Ancestor, since you have already become a fifth-grade Invincible, you should have visited the Eternal World known as the Tianlin Realm. I am a member of the Nether Corridor, a super-tier power in the Tianlin Realm. The Nether Corridor possesses many second-grade and third-grade Invincibles, ranking within the top hundred among the countless super-tier powers in the Tianlin Realm. Have you thought it through? Are you willing to offend such a colossus for a small opportunity?"
...
Ancestor Mingli Mist did not want to fight Ye Tian, so he brought up the Nether Corridor to intimidate him.
However.
Ye Tian gave a cold laugh and said, "Nether Corridor? Is it very powerful? I happen to be a high-level member of the Tianfeng Sea!"
"The Saint-tier Tianfeng Sea? Don't try to fool me!" Ancestor Mingli Mist didn't believe Ye Tian's words at all.
At that moment, Ye Tian took out his badge belonging to the Tianfeng Sea and said, "This is my Tianfeng Sea badge. If you still don't believe it, then it doesn't matter. In short, today you must die!"
Ancestor Mingli Mist started to believe him, but he wouldn't admit it.
Moreover, it was impossible for him to give up this opportunity.
"Wanfa Ancestor should have only just ascended to a fifth-grade Invincible. Furthermore, the Yuhua World is currently not in a Great Tribulation period, so he is being suppressed by the world's rules. His strength is greatly diminished; I still have hope of winning!" Ancestor Mingli Mist thought to himself.
Immediately, he made his move!
Ye Tian also moved at the same time.
As soon as he struck, Ye Tian unleashed a top-tier Invincible Ancestral Technique—the Heavenly Pole Combat Technique.
Kill!!!!!
Boom!!!!
The void trembled as the two fifth-grade Invincibles immediately clashed in a life-and-death struggle.
The moment they engaged, Ye Tian discovered that Ancestor Mingli Mist's Invincible Tribulation Body was too fragile, far inferior to his own.
Clearly, Ancestor Mingli Mist had never cultivated an Invincible Tribulation Body manual, which was why he was so fragile.
Even though Ye Tian was suppressed by the rules of the Yuhua World and could only exert a small portion of his strength, he still easily crushed Ancestor Mingli Mist.
After a few moves, Ancestor Mingli Mist's Invincible Tribulation Body was blasted apart by Ye Tian.


Warm Reminder: If you can't find the book by its title, you can try searching by the author's name. It might have just been renamed!

Chapter 1549: Xumi Golden Mountain, Xumi Golden Fruit!

Chapter 1549: Xumi Golden Mountain, Xumi Golden Fruit!

"Your Invincible Tribulation Body is actually this powerful!"
Ming Li Fog Ancestor’s entire body trembled.
His Invincible Tribulation Body had just been blasted apart once, and nearly thirty percent of his physical body had been annihilated. If this continued, he would soon perish.
Both were fifth-grade Invincibles, and he had been a fifth-grade Invincible for countless ages, possessing strength far greater than an average fifth-grade Invincible and having comprehended two Invincible Techniques. He never expected to be so far inferior to Ye Tian.
It was evident how terrifyingly powerful Ye Tian's Invincible Tribulation Body was, far exceeding his imagination.
Furthermore, the Invincible Technique Ye Tian performed was definitely no ordinary technique, but a top-tier Invincible Technique. Thus, the power it unleashed far surpassed his own.
Had Ye Tian not been suppressed by the rules of the Feathered Heaven, only able to exert a small fraction of his strength, Ming Li Fog Ancestor would have been killed instantly.
"Escape!" Ming Li Fog Ancestor was no longer prepared to guard this opportunity. No matter how great the opportunity, if he perished, everything would be for naught.
However, he simply could not escape.
Ye Tian had no intention of letting him go, and he had no time at all to break through the barrier of the Feathered Heaven.
Soon, Ming Li Fog Ancestor’s life force was completely annihilated, turning into a corpse that floated above the golden mountain.
The battle just now had not caused even a shred of damage to the golden mountain, which was enough to show the miraculous nature of this place.
Ye Tian felt no pride in slaying a fifth-grade Invincible like Ming Li Fog Ancestor.
In reality, Ming Li Fog Ancestor was quite weak. Though he seemed to have comprehended two Invincible Techniques, both his foundation and his Invincible Tribulation Body were incredibly fragile. Any random fifth-grade Invincible from the Tianfeng Sea could easily crush him.
Therefore, killing such a fifth-grade Invincible naturally required little effort.
Swish!
Ye Tian arrived at Ming Li Fog Ancestor’s palace on the golden mountain. There wasn't much inside; it was merely a simple residence.
Subsequently, Ye Tian found a golden scroll among Ming Li Fog Ancestor’s belongings. This golden scroll recorded a piece of information.
Xumi Golden Mountain: Ranked 128th among Eternal Source Objects. One Xumi Golden Fruit is born every thirty thousand Kalpa Eras. Consuming the Xumi Golden Fruit can strengthen the physical body, condense the soul, and permanently enhance comprehension.
"It’s actually the Xumi Golden Fruit!"
Ye Tian was immensely shocked.
During his years in the Tianfeng Sea, he hadn't just been cultivating bitterly; he had also learned about various treasures through the Tianfeng Sea, and the Xumi Golden Fruit was among them.
However, high-level members were not qualified to exchange for the Xumi Golden Fruit; only elite members had that privilege.
According to his understanding, a single Xumi Golden Fruit required one billion contribution points.
If one point of contribution from the Tianfeng Sea were converted into Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, it would be equivalent to at least 4,000 crystals, and likely even more.
This was because Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals were easy to obtain, but they couldn't be used to exchange for many rare treasures, whereas Tianfeng Sea contribution points could.
Therefore, what did one billion contribution points represent? It was equivalent to trillions of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals!
For Ming Li Fog Ancestor and the Blood Mist Alliance, their entire net worth was likely far less than a hundred million Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals. It was clear how massive the attraction of the Xumi Golden Fruit was to them.
Whether they traded it away or refined it themselves, it was an unimaginable opportunity.
Unfortunately, all of this now belonged to Ye Tian.
"No wonder Ming Li Fog Ancestor was unwilling to leave. Who would give up a treasure worth trillions of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals? Moreover, the Xumi Golden Fruit is just one type of treasure produced by the Xumi Golden Mountain. The value of the mountain itself is even greater, simply incalculable. If it were me, I wouldn't be able to abandon this place either!" Ye Tian thought to himself.
The Xumi Golden Mountain was an Eternal Source Object. Ye Tian had some knowledge of Eternal Source Objects; though limited, he knew they were higher in tier than Rule Heavenly Objects.
Rule Heavenly Objects were treasures born from an Eternal Heaven, representing its rules. However, Eternal Source Objects corresponded to the Source Sea. Most Eternal Source Objects were born within the Source Sea. Once they appeared, even the lowliest Eternal Source Object would trigger a bloodbath among numerous first-grade Invincibles.
And if a powerful Eternal Source Object emerged, perhaps even Supreme Beings would take action.
An Eternal Source Object like the Xumi Golden Mountain was something even the Tianfeng Sea might not be able to protect.
"This kind of treasure cannot be reported. Furthermore, I had best completely seal off the Feathered Heaven. Otherwise, if word leaks out like it did for Ming Li Fog Ancestor today, it will be disastrous!"
Ye Tian thought secretly.
Completely sealing off an alien heaven was possible, but it required paying a heavy price...
Ye Tian currently had no way to completely seal an alien heaven, so he had his Invincible Progenitor Avatar descend into the Feathered Heaven to stand guard there.
Later, through research, Ye Tian discovered that the day of the Xumi Golden Fruit's birth was not far off.
"In six Dark Eras at most, the Xumi Golden Fruit will appear!" Ye Tian estimated.
This was the maximum time; it was also possible it could be born in the next second.
After all, it was an Eternal Source Object, so there was no way to estimate accurately.
It had to be said that Ming Li Fog Ancestor simply lacked luck; he perished just as the Xumi Golden Fruit was about to be born.
Time passed slowly, and in the blink of an eye, five Dark Eras had gone by.
During this time, Ye Tian made great progress.
With ample resources, he raised his cultivation to the limit of a fifth-grade Invincible. He also cultivated the Invincible Tribulation Body technique, "Ten Thousand Origins Returning to the Void," to the late stage of the second layer. After refining and perfecting it, his main body finally reached the late stage of the second layer of Ten Thousand Origins Returning to the Void.
However, going from the late stage of the second layer to full completion would likely take another full Kalpa Era.
On this day.
The Xumi Golden Fruit was born!
Hum!!!!
Upon the Xumi Golden Mountain, an illusory golden fruit appeared.
Just like the Xumi Golden Mountain itself, divine sense and other methods could not detect it; it could only be seen with the naked eye.
As time passed, the Xumi Golden Fruit absorbed the power of the Xumi Golden Mountain and slowly became solid.
After approximately several hundred million years, this Xumi Golden Fruit finally matured.
Immediately, Ye Tian plucked the fruit.
Now, Ye Tian had two choices. The first was to hand the Xumi Golden Fruit over to the Tianfeng Sea, which would net him at least ten million contribution points.
However, if he did that, the Xumi Golden Mountain could no longer be kept a secret.
Furthermore, he wasn't currently lacking contribution points, and with his abilities, earning them wasn't difficult.
Therefore, he would not choose that path.
"I'll just eat it directly!"
Ye Tian decided.
Immediately, he brought the Xumi Golden Fruit back to the Dark Forbidden Zone and had his main body swallow it in one gulp.
